[15/08/25, 11:42:59 AM] Sanket Office: Everyone Read this 



📢 Important Announcement: Payment Collection Process

If a rider generates a payment link but does not complete the payment, please follow the steps below:

Wait for 20 minutes after the payment link is generated.

During this time, decide whether:

The rider will complete the payment via the link, OR

You will collect the payment manually and pay it from FO via Razorpay or CMS.

Do not use both methods at the same time.

To avoid delays and confusion, always choose only one method to clear the pending amount — either via Kaptaan payment link or manual payment from FO via Razorpay/CMS.

Please ensure this process is followed strictly for smooth and timely operations.

Thank you,
Sanket Choudhary
